[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEncoding Rules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m dissector. The AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m report indicates a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnamed [0m[32m'name_string'[0m[39m in the `try_dissect_unknown_ber` function. The overflow occurs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring the execution of `dissect_ber_GeneralString` at line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m of packet-ber.c.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability classified as a write operation. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSCARINESS score is [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, indicating a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow. This type [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof vulnerability occurs when data is written beyond the allocated boundaries of a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-based buffer.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during fuzzing of the BER handler dissector with the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing characteristics:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location of Overflow**: The overflow occurs in the `dissect_ber_GeneralString`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at line [0m[1;92m3194:34[0m[39m of `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-ber.c[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Stack Frame Analysis**: The ASan report identifies that the problematic memory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess occurs in the `try_dissect_unknown_ber` function's stack frame, which [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontains [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m stack-allocated objects. The critical buffer is:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `name_string` at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - an [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The memory access occurs at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, which is one byte before the start of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39munderflow[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Call Stack**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following call chain:[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `call_all_postdissectors`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Layout**: The shadow bytes around the buggy address show:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The access at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m is marked as `f2` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mStack mid redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This indicates the write occurred in the red zone area between stack [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables, specifically one byte before the `name_string` buffer[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactx, tree, tvb, offset, hf_id, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? &out_tvb : NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3188[0m[39m:            tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3189[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3195[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3196[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3199[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-ber.[0m[1;92mc:1779[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1780[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1779[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1780[0m[39m:            *out_tvb = [0m[1;35mber_tvb_new_subset_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified a critical[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow vulnerability in the `dissect_ber_GeneralString` function at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[39m of `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Causes[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability stems from two interconnected bugs:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Incorrect Length Retrieval [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code reads `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` from the original [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket tvbuff at an arbitrary offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter BER headers have been parsed[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It should instead read the length from `out_tvb`, which contains the extracted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring data[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With malicious input [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this results in reading [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m as the length[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Unbounded Array Write [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code writes `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;` without verifying `tvb_len < [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname_len`[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `tvb_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m exceeds `name_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this writes [0m[1;36m175[0m[39m bytes beyond the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer bounds[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This causes the stack-buffer-overflow detected by AddressSanitizer[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type Mismatch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3177[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `tvb_len` is declared as `int8_t` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but should be unsigned to properly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandle tvbuff lengths[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Context[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase contains two implementations of `dissect_ber_GeneralString`:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **First implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Dead code using undefined constant [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BER_UNI_TAG_GENSTR` - cannot compile[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Second implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Active implementation with the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe active implementation calls `dissect_ber_restricted_string`, which creates [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`out_tvb` as a subset tvbuff containing only the extracted string data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ber_tvb_new_subset_length` at line [0m[1;36m1780[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The proper way to get the length of this[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracted data is through `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which is the pattern used[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., line [0m[1;36m1497[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix the Active Implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the `dissect_ber_GeneralString` function to:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Change variable type [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3177[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace `int8_t tvb_len;` with `unsigned tvb_len;`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This matches the return type of `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and prevents [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msign-related issues[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fix length retrieval [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This reads the actual length of the extracted string from the correct tvbuff[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fix null terminator placement [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m3194[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The current code writes `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;` unconditionally[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This must be moved inside the conditional branches to ensure bounds checking[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `tvb_len >= name_len`, write at `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mname_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `tvb_len < name_len`, write at `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msafe[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe corrected logic for lines [0m[1;36m3177[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned tvb_len;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed from int8_t[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset = [0m[1;35mdissect_ber_restricted_string[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse, BER_UNI_TAG_GeneralString, actx, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtree, tvb, offset, hf_id, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? &out_tvb : NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Get length from extracted data[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mname_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Terminate within bounds[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Safe: tvb_len < name_len[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove Dead Code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe first implementation of `dissect_ber_GeneralString` should be removed because:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It references undefined constant `BER_UNI_TAG_GENSTR` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshould be [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BER_UNI_TAG_GeneralString`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It has a different function signature [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`int name_len` vs `unsigned name_len`[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It's not the function declared in the header file [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.h:[0m[1;36m147[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It cannot compile or run in its current state[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis cleanup prevents future confusion and maintenance issues.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Addresses the Root Cause**: Fixes the incorrect tvb and offset usage that [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleads to reading arbitrary packet data as the string length[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: Maintains the same conditional copy logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3189[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3193[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that properly bounds-checks the `tvb_memcpy` operation[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Codebase Patterns**: Uses `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` consistently with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother parts of the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., line [0m[1;36m1497[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1504[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Type Safety**: Changes `int8_t` to `unsigned` to match the API return type and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent sign-related bugs[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only modifies the buggy lines without affecting the broader[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector chain or fuzzing infrastructure[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Functionality[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The dissection chain [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_ber_restricted_string` → [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_constrained_restricted_string` → [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_constrained_octet_string`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `out_tvb` creation and management remain unchanged[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The conditional logic for copying data is preserved[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only the length retrieval and null termination are corrected[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **String Truncation**: If the extracted string is longer than `name_len-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, it [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill be truncated[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is expected behavior; the caller provides a fixed-size [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer and the function respects those bounds[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This matches the behavior of the old implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: Using `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of `[0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmight have minimal performance impact[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The function call overhead is negligible compared to the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissection work[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is the correct API usage pattern throughout Wireshark[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Null Termination Position**: The null terminator position changes for strings [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat exceed buffer size[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the correct behavior; strings must be null-terminated [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin allocated bounds[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This prevents buffer overflows in downstream code that uses the string[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the pattern used in the first [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdead code[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m implementation:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[39m: Proper bounds checking before using `len`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m3094[0m[39m: Safe null termination after bounds checking[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAnd matches tvbuff usage patterns throughout packet-ber.c:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1497[0m[39m: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m1504[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
